	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Shania Twain</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">"Shania" redirects here. For the given name, see <a href="/wiki/Shania_(given_name)" title="Shania (given name)">Shania (given name)</a>.</div>
<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Canadian recording artist; country pop singer and songwriter</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<table class="infobox biography vcard" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold"><div class="fn" style="display:inline">Shania Twain</div><br /><div class="honorific-suffix" style="font-size: 77%; font-weight: normal; display:inline;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">OC</a></div></th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><a href="/wiki/File:ShaniaTwainJunoAwardsMar2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="ShaniaTwainJunoAwardsMar2011.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/ShaniaTwainJunoAwardsMar2011.jpg/220px-ShaniaTwainJunoAwardsMar2011.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="347" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/ee/ShaniaTwainJunoAwardsMar2011.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="325" data-file-height="513" /></a><div>Twain at the 2011 Juno Awards</div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Born</th><td><div style="display:inline" class="nickname">Eilleen Regina Edwards</div><br /><span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday">1965-08-28</span>) </span>August 28, 1965<span class="noprint ForceAgeToShow"> (age&#160;54)</span><br /><div style="display:inline" class="birthplace"><a href="/wiki/Windsor,_Ontario" title="Windsor, Ontario">Windsor, Ontario</a>, Canada</div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Occupation</th><td class="role"><div class="hlist hlist-separated"><ul><li>Singer</li><li>songwriter</li><li>actress</li></ul></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap">Spouse(s)</span></th><td><div style="display:inline-block;line-height:normal;margin:2px 0px;"><a href="/wiki/Robert_John_%22Mutt%22_Lange" title="Robert John &quot;Mutt&quot; Lange">Robert John "Mutt" Lange</a><br />&#40;<abbr title="married">m.</abbr>&#160;1993&#59;&#32;<abbr title="divorced">div.</abbr>&#160;2010&#41;</div><br /><div style="display:inline-block;line-height:normal;margin:2px 0px;">Frédéric Thiébaud<br />&#32;&#40;<abbr title="married">m.</abbr>&#160;2011&#41;</div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Children</th><td>1</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><b>Musical career</b></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Origin</th><td><a href="/wiki/Timmins" title="Timmins">Timmins</a>, Ontario, Canada</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Genres</th><td><div class="hlist hlist-separated"><ul><li><a href="/wiki/Country_music" title="Country music">Country</a></li><li><a href="/wiki/Country_pop" title="Country pop">country pop</a></li><li><a href="/wiki/Country_rock" title="Country rock">country rock</a></li><li><a href="/wiki/Pop_music" title="Pop music">pop</a></li></ul></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Instruments</th><td class="note"><div class="hlist hlist-separated"><ul><li>Vocals</li><li>guitar</li></ul></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row"><span class="nowrap">Years active</span></th><td>1983–present</td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Labels</th><td><a href="/wiki/Universal_Music_Group_Nashville" title="Universal Music Group Nashville">Mercury Nashville</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row">Website</th><td><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://shaniatwain.com">shaniatwain<wbr />.com</a></span></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Shania Twain</b>, <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">OC</a> (<span class="nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="/ʃ/: &#39;sh&#39; in &#39;shy&#39;">ʃ</span><span title="/ə/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">ə</span><span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">ˈ</span><span title="&#39;n&#39; in &#39;nigh&#39;">n</span><span title="/aɪ/: &#39;i&#39; in &#39;tide&#39;">aɪ</span><span title="/./: syllable break">.</span><span title="/ə/: &#39;a&#39; in &#39;about&#39;">ə</span></span>/</a></span></span>; born <b>Eilleen Regina Edwards</b>; August 28, 1965) is a Canadian singer, songwriter and actress. She has sold over 100 million records, making her the best-selling female artist in country music history and among the <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_music_artists" title="List of best-selling music artists">best-selling music artists of all time</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Her success garnered her several honorific titles including the "<a href="/wiki/Honorific_nicknames_in_popular_music" title="Honorific nicknames in popular music">Queen of Country Pop</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Raised in <a href="/wiki/Timmins,_Ontario" class="mw-redirect" title="Timmins, Ontario">Timmins, Ontario</a>, Twain pursued singing and songwriting from a young age before signing with <a href="/wiki/Universal_Music_Group_Nashville" title="Universal Music Group Nashville">Mercury Nashville Records</a> in the early 1990s. Her <a href="/wiki/Shania_Twain_(album)" title="Shania Twain (album)">self-titled debut studio album</a> saw little commercial success upon release in 1993. After collaborating with producer and later husband <a href="/wiki/Robert_John_%22Mutt%22_Lange" title="Robert John &quot;Mutt&quot; Lange">Robert John "Mutt" Lange</a>, Twain rose to fame with her second studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Woman_in_Me_(Shania_Twain_album)" title="The Woman in Me (Shania Twain album)">The Woman in Me</a></i> (1995), which brought her widespread success. It sold 20 million copies worldwide, spawned widely successful singles such as "<a href="/wiki/Any_Man_of_Mine" title="Any Man of Mine">Any Man of Mine</a>", and earned her a <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award" title="Grammy Award">Grammy Award</a>. Her third studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Come_On_Over" title="Come On Over">Come On Over</a></i> (1997), became the <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_albums" title="List of best-selling albums">best-selling studio album</a> of all time by a female act in any genre and the best-selling country album, selling nearly 40 million copies worldwide.<sup id="cite_ref-News124_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-News124-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> <i>Come On Over</i> produced twelve singles, including "<a href="/wiki/You%27re_Still_the_One" title="You&#39;re Still the One">You're Still the One</a>", "<a href="/wiki/From_This_Moment_On_(Shania_Twain_song)" title="From This Moment On (Shania Twain song)">From This Moment On</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/Man!_I_Feel_Like_a_Woman!" title="Man! I Feel Like a Woman!">Man! I Feel Like a Woman!</a>", and earned Twain four Grammy Awards. Her fourth studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Up!_(album)" title="Up! (album)">Up!</a></i> (2002), was also <a href="/wiki/RIAA_certification" title="RIAA certification">certified Diamond</a> in the United States.
</p><p>In 2004, Twain entered a hiatus, revealing years later that diagnoses with <a href="/wiki/Lyme_disease" title="Lyme disease">Lyme disease</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dysphonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Dysphonia">dysphonia</a> led to a severely weakened singing voice.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In 2011, she chronicled her vocal rehabilitation on the <a href="/wiki/Oprah_Winfrey_Network_(U.S._TV_channel)" class="mw-redirect" title="Oprah Winfrey Network (U.S. TV channel)">OWN</a> miniseries <i><a href="/wiki/Why_Not%3F_with_Shania_Twain" title="Why Not? with Shania Twain">Why Not? with Shania Twain</a>,</i> released her first single in six years, "<a href="/wiki/Today_Is_Your_Day" title="Today Is Your Day">Today Is Your Day</a>", and published an autobiography, <i>From This Moment On</i>. Twain returned to performing the following year with an exclusive <a href="/wiki/Concert_residency" title="Concert residency">concert residency</a> at <a href="/wiki/The_Colosseum_at_Caesars_Palace" title="The Colosseum at Caesars Palace">The Colosseum at Caesars Palace</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/Shania:_Still_the_One" title="Shania: Still the One">Shania: Still the One</a></i>, which ran until 2014. In 2015, she launched the North American <a href="/wiki/Rock_This_Country_Tour" title="Rock This Country Tour">Rock This Country Tour</a>, which was billed as her farewell tour.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Twain released her first studio album in 15 years in 2017, <i><a href="/wiki/Now_(Shania_Twain_album)" title="Now (Shania Twain album)">Now</a></i>, and embarked on the <a href="/wiki/Shania_Now_Tour" class="mw-redirect" title="Shania Now Tour">Shania Now Tour</a> in 2018.
</p><p>Twain has received five <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award" title="Grammy Award">Grammy Awards</a>, 27 <a href="/wiki/Broadcast_Music,_Inc." title="Broadcast Music, Inc.">BMI</a> Songwriter Awards, stars on <a href="/wiki/Canada%27s_Walk_of_Fame" title="Canada&#39;s Walk of Fame">Canada's Walk of Fame</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame" title="Hollywood Walk of Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</a>, and an induction into the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Music_Hall_of_Fame" title="Canadian Music Hall of Fame">Canadian Music Hall of Fame</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> According to the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">RIAA</a> she is the only female artist in history to have three (consecutive) albums <a href="/wiki/RIAA_certification" title="RIAA certification">certified Diamond</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">RIAA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> and is the <a href="/wiki/List_of_highest-certified_music_artists_in_the_United_States" title="List of highest-certified music artists in the United States">sixth best-selling female artist</a> is the United States. Altogether, Twain is ranked as the 10th best-selling artist of the <a href="/wiki/Nielsen_SoundScan" title="Nielsen SoundScan">Nielsen SoundScan</a> era.<sup id="cite_ref-Ref_b_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ref_b-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
